Sean mentioned that he grew up in Crystal Lake and a bad tornado gave him an intense fear of them (lilapsophobia). I remember being with friends in Johnsburg (about 14 miles from Crystal Lake) when the most traumatic experience of my life up to that time occurred. In 1989 a tornado ripped through a small park adjacent to my friend's backyard. It bent solid metal swingsets, sent the tilt-o-whirl flying into the woods, and tore out the chain link fence like it was a row of toothpicks. From that moment on and for the next five years, I had a panic attack any time the weather looked a little bleak. Living in McHenry County will do that to you.
